&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;To repeat, there will be four ‚Äî count ‚Äôem ‚Äî four days of deals aimed at Prime subscribers, which means you have double the amount of time to save this year. <!-- TECH_JOBS:START --><div class="content-card jobs"><span class="tag">JOBS</span><h3><a href="https://remoteOK.com/remote-jobs/remote-partnerships-lead-espresso-1093557">Partnerships Lead</a></h3><p class="desc">&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12pt;&quot;&gt;Espresso Systems is the lead developer of Espresso, a global confirmation layer designed to enhance cross-chain composability by providing fast and reliable transaction confirmations. Espresso confirmations help reduce finality risk and prevent issues like sequencer equivocation, making it easier for applications to operate across multiple chains. The network is currently in its Mainnet 0 release and supports various functionalities, including fast confirmations, decentralized sequencing, and low-cost data availability.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12pt;&quot;&gt;At Espresso Systems, we work with leading teams developing chains, rollups, and applications including Offchain Labs, Polygon, Cartesi, RARI Chain, and beyond√¢¬Ä¬îall united in our mission to build an open experience in which all chains work together as one.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12pt;&quot;&gt;The Espresso team comprises a diverse and passionate group of contributors from around the world. We are developers, designers, and researchers who have contributed in academia, in open source communities, in policymaking, and beyond. We are backed by over $50m in funding from leading investors in technology and crypto including a16z, Greylock Partners, Electric Capital, Sequoia Capital, and Polychain Capital.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 12pt;&quot;&gt;As Partnerships Lead, you will be driving adoption of Espresso technology, delivering integrations with emerging app developer teams and enterprise blockchain studios alike. ## How It Works
This content is automatically updated using [blog-post-workflow](https://github.com/gautamkrishnar/blog-post-workflow), which fetches the latest content from various RSS feeds and updates this README.

## Usage for LinkedIn
The content cards above can be copied directly for use in LinkedIn posts. Each card includes:
- A headline
- A brief description
- A link to the full article
- Publication date

## Customize
To customize the feeds or layout, edit the `.github/workflows/content-aggregator.yml` file.
